msg:I came to Tiantai for a two-day weekend vacation and stayed at Xingye. The hotel's hardware is comfortable and the staff training is in place. From driving to the hotel, because the hotel's new energy charging procedure is a bit complicated, the young man in the luggage depar**ent is very enthusiastic to help operate and explain. When checking in, Miss Chen at the front desk is also amiable and responsible. She is service-minded but does not disturb the guests. The waiters in the restaurant can also introduce the dishes and confirm with the guests. The front desk staff responds to any inquiries from the guests very quickly and efficiently. The way from the lobby to the room is a bit like a maze. Once I got confused and went to the lobby to ask, and the young man sent me directly to the room.
In terms of the hotel's service, you can feel that the training has taken a lot of effort in the details. It is serving guests attentively.
For breakfast, although many guests complained that it was simple, I can accept this set meal format. It's just that in the Japanese set meal, the quality of rice is slightly improved (the Japanese are very particular about the quality of rice. There is a proverb "As long as there is delicious rice and pickles, every day is a good day."), the side dishes are not pickles, and they are replaced with big roots, etc., which may be more Japanese.
The makeup artist and photographer for the travel photography provided by the hotel were very responsible and took good photos.
Finally, I want to say that in recent weeks, I have been staying in hotels with gold diamond level on Ctrip and Qunar.com in Suzhou. Only international chain hotels, such as Four Seasons and Hoshino in Suzhou, will not ask guests to write five-star reviews when they leave the hotel. Others will all make such requests in a tactful way. Some will even send WeChat push notifications after the guests leave the hotel.
In the future, when I come to Tiantai, Hoshino will be my first choice.

We stayed here for three nights on the eighth day of the ***** New Year and prayed at Guoqing Temple! The short four days left us with the best memories, top-notch service, kindness and warmth, and meticulous attention to detail!

A top-notch beautiful hotel on the top of a mountain 800 meters above sea level. Every corner is precise and elegant. I am amazed by the symmetry of oriental beauty! From the lobby, restaurant, swimming pool, to the symmetrical beauty everywhere in the guest rooms, the designer loves and adheres to the central axis of symmetry so much, and has grasped the Chinese life aesthetics to the highest level. Vacationing is like being in an art school.

A top Zen hotel at the top of a mountain 800 meters above sea level, you can enjoy the mountain view from a distance in the lobby bar, enjoy all-day tea breaks in the Yangyun Pond that blends with the sky, overlook the rolling mountains, and learn Baduanjin! Meditate! There are more than 1,500 volumes of Sikuquanshu in the bookstore. This kind of vacation makes people quiet, extremely comfortable, and cultivates their mind!

A very good-looking hotel that looks great even when you take pictures with your mobile phone! The hotel provides free travel photography, and ancient costumes allow you to travel through history and become a classic beauty. Because we were going to Shiliang Scenic Area, I wore my own red coat and took the photo without makeup. The photographer‚Äôs superb skills, in the digital age, he still clicked the shutter once for each photo and completed it in 15 minutes‚úÖ, I admire it!

With a Zen mind, eating well is practice! The hotel's restaurant is truly delicious, and the super attentive service impressed me. The garlic bean noodles are what the gods eat. The garlic bean noodles made in the hotel‚Äôs Chinese restaurant are so delicious that we must order them with every meal!

The hotel is located among the beautiful mountains and rivers of Tiantai Mountain in Zhejiang. It is very convenient to go to Guoqing Temple and Shiliang Scenic Area. You don‚Äôt have to worry about the inconvenience of transportation when staying on the mountain. The hotel will help guests book vehicles. Everything is the best arrangement! I will come again!

msg:The hotel is located in the upper mountains. When the weather is good, the winding mountain road is easy to drive. When we went there, we encountered rime and heavy fog. Although the trip was disrupted, the children and we were very happy with the rare beauty.
The hotel is located in the middle of the country, close to the ski resort. It takes about fifteen minutes to go to Shiliang, and less than half an hour to go down the mountain to Guoqing. There are other ways to go to different attractions, but I will not comment.
The hygiene is beyond reproach. The rooms, bathrooms, corridors, restaurants, swimming pools and gyms are all very clean, and water and other supplies are available everywhere.
In terms of hardware, it is quite nice. The hotel is quite new, the bathroom facilities are very useful, and the bedding is comfortable. There are many small gardens in the Chinese style garden. It was freezing that day and I didn‚Äôt explore much, but I can see that the design is very thoughtful.
The best thing about the hotel is the service. I added WeChat in advance to guide the route and arrange meals. When I went out to watch the snow in the middle of the night, the front desk security guard helped find an umbrella. The front desk service, catering waiters and swimming pool waiters were all very polite and enthusiastic. Because it is foggy, snowy and freezing, every waiter you meet will remind you to pay attention to your safety even outside the hotel.
The breakfast is semi-buffet, you can fill up and eat well. There are three choices of vegetarian, Japanese and Chinese, all of which are delicious; the breakfast service in the restaurant is great.
Generally speaking, it is a pretty good five-star hotel, suitable for vacation;
Having said that, here are some comments:
1. The hotel has insufficient entertainment facilities. There are only swimming pools and gyms. If you are stuck in the hotel with your baby, you have nothing to do, and there is nothing in Lotus Town. Why can't we open some arts and crafts, painting, children's activity rooms, etc.? There is no SAP, no chess and cards, no KTV, and no place for adults to go. It felt like I could only live in the place and go out to play during the day;
2. What I am least satisfied with or want to complain about is the price of catering, which is extremely low value for money. Dinner that day and dinner the next day are 1200-1300 each time! I don‚Äôt dare to order the food. Although the products are good, the price/performance ratio is so good. Your so-called hand-caught hairtail fish, which is so skinny as a stick, sells for 300+ for 6 pieces! ! I think it was the biggest failure of this trip, and it even affected my mood. I wanted to complain to your restaurant at that time! Take a look at Figure 9 in the photo for yourself!
Overall, the environmental facilities, sanitation and services are pretty good. You can stay here, but don‚Äôt miss lunch or dinner!

Officially wrote 50 square meters, but there should be no balcony.
In addition, some bathrooms have washing power and some do not.
The spare parts are general. The toothbrush is the kind that sheds hair while brushing.
Hotel breakfast is worth complaining for ten minutes
Set meal system + buffet The buffet selection is simple salad‚ûï bread, fruit, and some Japanese-style miso soup and rice. There are few varieties. The set menu has Japanese, Chinese, and Western options. To be honest, the dishes are very disappointing. They are stylish but not quality. In addition, due to the large number of people living, there are often no food but there is no way to supplement the situation.
There are more than 100 rooms in the hotel, and 50 rooms are opened. The service staff is still insufficiently equipped. When eating breakfast, you will feel that there is an obvious shortage of staff. Also due to lack of staff, some rooms have turndown service, some do not.
The above is the inadequacy, because it is a brand known for hotel services, which will have higher requirements for the hotel
If it is only a five-star hotel, the above problems may not be a big problem, but if it is true, there is no sense of expectation.
